	// remove / add default data function
	function clear_input2(elID, newValue){
		
		if($(elID).value == newValue) $(elID).value = "";
	}
	function unClear_input2(elID, newValue) {
		
		if($(elID).value == '') $(elID).value = newValue;
	}

<script type="text/javascript">
	
	Array.prototype.inArray = function (value,caseSensitive)
	// Returns true if the passed value is found in the
	// array. Returns false if it is not.
	{
		var i;
		for (i=0; i < this.length; i++) {
			// use === to check for Matches. ie., identical (===),
			if(caseSensitive){	//performs match even the string is case sensitive
				if (this[i].toLowerCase() == value.toLowerCase()) {
					return true;
				}
			}
			else {
				if (this[i] == value) {
					return true;
				}
			}
		}
		return false;
	};
	
	// Super Search Submit 
	function autopartsSearchFormSubmit() {
		
		//alert('Success! Submitted form data.');
		$j('#begin_searching_results_box').html('<em>Searching... Please Wait...</em>');
		$j('#autoparts_search_submit').html('Searching...');
		setTimeout(function() { 
			//document.autoparts_search.submit();
			$j('#autoparts_search_secret_submit').click();
		}, 60);
		return false; 
	}
	
	// Reset Search From 
	function autopartsSearchFormReset() {
		
		//document.autoparts_search.reset();
		$j('#autoparts_search_secret_reset').click();
		setTimeout(function() { changeOptionSet(); }, 60);
		return false; 
	}
	
	// Change Current Selection On Form 
	function autopartsSearchChangeSelection() {
		
		var url = 'apps/sidebar_apps/autoparts_search/autoparts_search_inside.inc.php';
		
		new Ajax.Request(url,
		  {
			method:'get',  
			parameters: {
				reset_selection: 1
			},
			onLoading: function(){ 
			},
			onSuccess: function(transport){
				var response = transport.responseText || " No response text found, please try again ";
				$('autoparts_search_inside_area').innerHTML = response;	 
				autopartsSearchOnloads();
			},
			onFailure: function(){ 
				$('autoparts_search_inside_area').innerHTML = '<em>Sorry, there was an error with your request, please refresh the page and try again.</em>';
			}
		});
		return false;
	}
	
	// Change Options Set 
	var selectObj, url, nextSelect;
	function changeOptionSet(selectObj) {
		
		if(!selectObj || selectObj==undefined) {
			var selectObj = new Object();
		}
		if(!selectObj.title || selectObj.title==undefined) selectObj.title = 0;
		
		// Setup URL with existing form values added 
		url = 'apps/sidebar_apps/autoparts_search/options_result.json.php?options';
		url += $j('#autoparts_search').serialize();
					
		if(selectObj.title==4) {
			$j('#autoparts_search_submit').click(); // Submit Data
			return false;
		}
		else {
			
			$j('.autopartsSearchOptions[title='+ (parseFloat(selectObj.title)+1) + ']').each(function(i, nextSelect) {  
				
				//$j(nextSelect).html('<optgroup label="Please Select"><option value="">Select '+ nextSelect.id +'</option></optgroup>');
				nextSelect.setAttribute('disabled', 'disabled');
				
				// Set group of options to return 
				url += '&return_set_options=' + nextSelect.id;
				url += '&current_options_id=' + selectObj.title;
									
				setTimeout(function() {
					$j.getJSON(url, function(data) {
						
						// If data is empty
						if(data==null) {
							$j('#autoparts_search_submit').click(); // Submit Data
							return false;
						}
						
						// else if data is not empty 
						nextSelect.removeAttribute('disabled'); // <option value="">Select '+ nextSelect.id +'</option>
						$j(nextSelect).html('<optgroup label="Please Select">');
						$j(nextSelect)[0].options[0] = new Option('Select '+ nextSelect.id, '');
						
						var dropDownForYears = false;
						var eachYeararray = [];
						var nonFound = true;
						var foo = 0;
						var endArrayKey = 0;
						var startArrayKey = 9999;
						$j.each(data, function(i2,item) {								
							//$j(nextSelect).html(nextSelect.innerHTML + '<option value="' + item.value + '">' + item.text + '</option>'); 		
							
							if(item.value instanceof(Object)) {
								
								dropDownForYears = true; 
								var from = item.value.from; 
								var to = item.value.to; 
								for(i=from;i<=to;i++) {
									
									//if( ! eachYeararray.inArray(i) ) eachYeararray[foo] = i;
									if(i<startArrayKey) startArrayKey = i;
									if(i>endArrayKey) endArrayKey = i;
									eachYeararray[i] = i;
									foo++;
								}
								
							}
							else $j(nextSelect)[0].options[(i2+1)] = new Option(((item.value!='' && item.value!=' ') ? item.value : 'All' ), item.value);
							
							if((item.value!='') && (item.value!=' ')) nonFound = false;
						});
						
						//alert('start:'+startArrayKey);
						//alert('end:'+endArrayKey);
						
						if(dropDownForYears) {
							
							eachYeararray.sort(function(a,b)
							{
								return b - a; // Sorts to reverse order 
							});
							
							//for(i=0;i<=eachYeararray.length;i++) {
							foo = 0;
							for(i=startArrayKey;i<(endArrayKey+1);i++) { 
								if(eachYeararray[foo]) {
									$j(nextSelect)[0].options[(foo+1)] = new Option(eachYeararray[foo], eachYeararray[foo]);
								}
								foo++;
							}
						}
						
						if(nonFound && (nextSelect.title!=1) && (nextSelect.title!=0)) {
							$j('#autoparts_search_submit').click(); // Submit Data
							return false; 
						}
						else {
							//$(nextSelect).up(1).style.display = "table-row";
							if(jQuery.browser.msie) $(nextSelect).up().up().style.display='block';
							else $(nextSelect).up().up().style.display='table-row';
							$j(nextSelect).html(nextSelect.innerHTML + '</optgroup>');
						}
													
					});
				}, 10); 
			});
			$j('.autopartsSearchOptions').each(function(i, eachSelects) { 
				
				if(parseFloat(eachSelects.title) > (parseFloat(selectObj.title)+1) ) {
					$j(eachSelects).html('<optgroup label="Please Select"><option value="">Select '+ eachSelects.id +'</option></optgroup>');
					eachSelects.setAttribute('disabled', 'disabled');
				}
			});
		}
		
		selectObj = false;
	}
	
	// Onload selection for the autoparts search 
	function autopartsSearchOnloads() { 
		// Set all the autoparts select options onChange event to be the  
		$j('.autopartsSearchOptions').change(function() {				
			changeOptionSet(this);
		});
		
		$j('#autoparts_search_submit').click(function() {
			autopartsSearchFormSubmit();
			return false;
		});
		
		$j('#autoparts_search_reset').click(function() {
			autopartsSearchFormReset();
			return false;
		});
		
		$j('#autoparts_search_change_selection').click(function() {
			autopartsSearchChangeSelection();
			return false;
		});
		
		// Run Options Selector 
		changeOptionSet();
		
		// Make sure the buttons are showing...
		$j('#autoparts_search_submit').show();
		$j('#autoparts_search_reset').show();
	}
	
	// Onload of actual page 
	addNewOnload(function() {
		autopartsSearchOnloads();
	});
	
</script>

	var $j = jQuery.noConflict();
	
</script>

  		<!-- Additional Params -->

<h1>
     Beginning of Auto Tuning Store Performance Parts<span style="FONT-SIZE: medium"> </span></h1>
<p>
    <span style="FONT-SIZE: small">We are an Oakley, California based <a class="FCK__AnchorC" name="performance">performance</a> parts site that specializes in aftermarket car and truck parts and car accessories for American, Japanese and European vehicles. Since 2008, we have been providing both local and online customers with a wide range of products to help improve the performance and appearance of their vehicles. We have done so by working directly with many manufacturers and also many distributors to obtain the best assortment of products at reasonable prices. We have striven to accommodate our customers' performance needs by offering excellent customer service and competitive pricing on only the highest quality products, and Auto Tuning Store and its employees hope to provide the same experience for you.</span></p>
<p>
     </p>
<div class="clearfix">

<h3>
    <strong>Industry News</strong><img align="bottom" alt="Auto Tuning Store Performance Parts Social Media Links" height="13" src="http://www.autotuningstore.com/userfiles/images/auto-tuning-separator-flat.gif" title="Auto Tuning Store Performance Parts Social Media Links" width="726" />
</h3>

<h3>
     <img alt="Aftermarket Mechanic" src="http://www.autotuningstore.com/userfiles/images/Mechanic.jpg" style="BORDER-BOTTOM: 3px solid; BORDER-LEFT: 3px solid; WIDTH: 200px; FLOAT: left; HEIGHT: 200px; MARGIN-LEFT: 10px; BORDER-TOP: 3px solid; MARGIN-RIGHT: 10px; BORDER-RIGHT: 3px solid" />
    The Aftermarket Industry Overview
</h3>

<p>
    The motor vehicle aftermarket is a significant sector of the U.S. economy employing approximately 4.3 million people in 2008.  This industry encompasses all products and services purchased for light and heavy duty vehicles after the original sale including replacement parts, accessories, lubricants, appearance products, tires, collision repairs, service repairs as well as the tools and equipment necessary to make the repair.</p>
<p>
    Overall aftermarket sales totaled $280.7 billion in 2008, representing an increase of 0.2 percent over the previous year.  Sales in the automotive aftermarket totaled $210.2 billion while sales in the heavy duty vehicle aftermarket totaled $70.5 billion.</p>
<p class="clearfix">
     </p>
<h3>
     Do it yourself ideas</h3>
<p>
    Installing a <a class="FCK__AnchorC" name="cold_air_intake">cold air intake</a> is also a relatively simple and inexpensive (in many cases) project that is useful on many vehicles and can range anywhere from $150-$650. <img alt="Do it yourself ideas" src="http://www.autotuningstore.com/userfiles/images/Cold%20Air%20Intake.JPG" style="BORDER-BOTTOM: 3px solid; BORDER-LEFT: 3px solid; MARGIN-TOP: 5px; WIDTH: 240px; MARGIN-BOTTOM: 5px; FLOAT: right; HEIGHT: 180px; BORDER-TOP: 3px solid; BORDER-RIGHT: 3px solid" />A cold air intake system helps cool the air to your combustion chamber, resulting in more HP and occassionally better fuel economy. There are many manufacturers that make <a class="FCK__AnchorC" name="cold_air_intakes">cold air intakes</a>.  Some of the more prominent intakes are the <a class="FCK__AnchorC" name="afe_cold_air_intake">afe cold air intake</a>, <a class="FCK__AnchorC" name="kn_air_intake">kn air intake</a> and <a class="FCK__AnchorC" name="aem_air_intake">aem air intake</a>.  I use an <a class="FCK__AnchorC" name="injen_intake">injen intake</a> and it works wonderfully adding both power and increased fuel economy.  A <a class="FCK__AnchorC" name="short_ram_intake">short ram intake</a> is another option and is well liked because it stays in a boxed area in the engine bay eliminating the possibility of hydrolock which causes damage to your engine.</p>
<p>
    We invite you to check out our all <a href="/Blog.html">new blog</a>.  You might ask what makes our blog different from the thousands of other blogs on the internet now.  Our is written by gearheads and enthusiasts just like you.  In fact if you want to guest blog please contact us and we will see if we can come to an arrangement.  Many of the products that we sell will be highlighted in our blog.  New product releases, current affairs in the industry, racing news and much more will be featured.  If you are a fan of Import Tuner, Euro Tuner or other performance car magazines you will find alot of similar type of articles and posts.  Upcoming posts you have to look forward to are the new California Dreaming <strong><a href="/RKSport_Body_Kits--category--1190.html">RKSport Body Kits</a></strong>, How <strong><a href="/shop.php?p=each_manufacturers&id=319">Hyperwings Spoilers</a></strong> are chosen and a bio on <strong><a href="/shop.php?p=each_manufacturers&id=144">Competition Clutch</a></strong>.
</p>
